shim-dbg_15.4-0ubuntu1_arm64.deb
--------------------------------

 new Debian package, version 2.0.
 size 11964 bytes: control archive=840 bytes.
     768 bytes,    18 lines      control              
     220 bytes,     3 lines      md5sums              
 Package: shim-dbg
 Source: shim
 Version: 15.4-0ubuntu1
 Architecture: arm64
 Maintainer: Ubuntu Developers <ubuntu-devel-discuss@lists.ubuntu.com>
 Installed-Size: 32
 Depends: shim (= 15.4-0ubuntu1)
 Section: debug
 Priority: optional
 Description: boot loader to chain-load signed boot loaders under Secure Boot (dbg symbols)
  This package provides a minimalist boot loader which allows verifying
  signatures of other UEFI binaries against either the Secure Boot DB/DBX or
  against a built-in signature database.  Its purpose is to allow a small,
  infrequently-changing binary to be signed by the UEFI CA, while allowing
  an OS distributor to revision their main bootloader independently of the CA.
  .
  Debug symbols.
 Original-Maintainer: Steve Langasek <vorlon@debian.org>
